## Diagram 3

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    RunEventStart([run_event called]) --> BuildRequest[Build request_json with auth header]
    BuildRequest --> CreateContext[Create Lambda Context]
    CreateContext --> TryCall{Try lambda_handler}
    TryCall -->|Exception| HandleError[Print traceback]
    TryCall -->|Success| CheckStatus{Status code = 200?}
    HandleError --> ParseResponse
    CheckStatus --> ParseResponse[Parse response body JSON]
    ParseResponse --> ReturnJSON[Return response_json]
    ReturnJSON --> RunEventEnd([End])
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Main as main
    participant SE as simulate_events
    participant File as DATA_FILE
    participant RE as run_event
    participant LH as lambda_handler
    participant Counter as Counters
    
    Main->>SE: Call simulate_events
    SE->>File: Read lines
    File-->>SE: Return event lines
    SE->>SE: Initialize counters
    
    loop For each event
        SE->>SE: Parse JSON event
        alt Has queryStringParameters
            SE->>RE: run_event(query_string_params)
            RE->>RE: Build request_json
            RE->>LH: call(lambda_handler, request_json, context)
            LH-->>RE: response
            RE->>RE: Parse response body
            RE-->>SE: response_json
            
            alt Has etaDate
                SE->>SE: Extract new_eta and model_name
                SE->>SE: Calculate eta_diff
                SE->>SE: Calculate kpi_minutes_off
                SE->>Counter: Update counters
            end
        end
    end
    
    SE->>SE: Calculate averages
    SE->>Main: Print statistics
```
